`onEventTime()` 方法在注册的 event-time timer 触发时调用。\\n1053: * `onProcessingTime()` 方法在注册的 processing-time timer 触发时调用。\\n1054: * `onMerge()` 方法与有状态的 trigger 相关。该方法会在两个窗口合并时，\\n1055: 将窗口对应 trigger 的状态进行合并，比如使用会话窗口时。\\n1056: * 最后，`clear()` 方法处理在对应窗口被移除时所需的逻辑。\\n1057:      */\\n617:     public abstract class Context implements java.io.Serializable {\\n618:         /**\\n619: \",\"endLine\":619,\"startLine\":616},{\"content\":\"1125: \\n1126: ### Built-in and Custom Triggers\\n1127: \\n1128: Flink comes with a few built-in triggers.\\n1129: \\n1130: * The (already mentioned) `EventTimeTrigger` fires based on the progress of event-time as measured by watermarks.\\n1131: * The `ProcessingTimeTrigger` fires based on processing time.\\n1132: * The `CountTrigger` fires once the number of elements in a window exceeds the given limit.\\n1133: * The `PurgingTrigger` takes as argument another trigger and transforms it into a purging one.\\n1134: \\n1135: If you need to implement a custom trigger, you should check out the abstract\\n1136: {{< gh_link file=\\\"/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/Trigger.java\\\" name=\\\"Trigger\\\" >}} class.\\n1137: Please note that the API is still evolving and might change in future versions of Flink.\\n1138: \",\"endLine\":1138,\"startLine\":1125},{\"content\":\"1071: \\n1072: ## Triggers\\n1073: \\n1074: A `Trigger` determines when a window (as formed by the *window assigner*) is ready to be\\n1075: processed by the *window function*. Each `WindowAssigner` comes with a default `Trigger`.\\n1076: If the default trigger does not fit your needs, you can specify a custom trigger using `trigger(...)`.\\n1077: \\n1078: The trigger interface has five methods that allow a `Trigger` to react to different events:\\n1079: \\n1080: * The `onElement()` method is called for each element that is added to a window.\\n1081: * The `onEventTime()` method is called when  a registered event-time timer fires.\\n1082: * The `onProcessingTime()` method is called when a registered processing-time timer fires.\\n1083: * The `onMerge()` method is relevant for stateful triggers and merges the states of two triggers when their corresponding windows merge, *e.g.* when using session windows.\\n1084: * Finally the `clear()` method performs any action needed upon removal of the corresponding window.\\n1085: Triggers\n1044: \n1045: `Trigger` 决定了一个窗口（由 *window assigner* 定义）何时可以被 *window function* 处理。\n1046: 每个 `WindowAssigner` 都有一个默认的 `Trigger`。\n1047: 如果默认 trigger 无法满足你的需要，你可以在 `trigger(...)` 调用中指定自定义的 trigger。\n1048: \n1049: Trigger 接口提供了五个方法来响应不同的事件：\n1050: \n1051: * `onElement()` 方法在每个元素被加入窗口时调用。\n1052: * `onEventTime()` 方法在注册的 event-time timer 触发时调用。\n1053: * `onProcessingTime()` 方法在注册的 processing-time timer 触发时调用。\n1054: * `onMerge()` 方法与有状态的 trigger 相关。该方法会在两个窗口合并时，\n1055: 将窗口对应 trigger 的状态进行合并，比如使用会话窗口时。\n1056: * 最后，`clear()` 方法处理在对应窗口被移除时所需的逻辑。\n1057: ","endLine":1057,"startLine":1042}],"file":"docs/content.zh/docs/dev/datastream/operators/windows.md","repo":"github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc","type":"file","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/-/blob/docs/content.zh/docs/dev/datastream/operators/windows.md"},{"chunks":[{"content":"616:      */\n617:     public abstract class Context implements java.io.Serializable {\n618:         /**\n619: ","endLine":619,"startLine":616},{"content":"1125: \n1126: ### Built-in and Custom Triggers\n1127: \n1128: Flink comes with a few built-in triggers.\n1129: \n1130: * The (already mentioned) `EventTimeTrigger` fires based on the progress of event-time as measured by watermarks.\n1131: * The `ProcessingTimeTrigger` fires based on processing time.\n1132: * The `CountTrigger` fires once the number of elements in a window exceeds the given limit.\n1133: * The `PurgingTrigger` takes as argument another trigger and transforms it into a purging one.\n1134: \n1135: If you need to implement a custom trigger, you should check out the abstract\n1136: {{< gh_link file=\"/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/Trigger.java\" name=\"Trigger\" >}} class.\n1137: Please note that the API is still evolving and might change in future versions of Flink.\n1138: ","endLine":1138,"startLine":1125},{"content":"1071: \n1072: ## Triggers\n1073: \n1074: A `Trigger` determines when a window (as formed by the *window assigner*) is ready to be\n1075: processed by the *window function*. Each `WindowAssigner` comes with a default `Trigger`.\n1076: If the default trigger does not fit your needs, you can specify a custom trigger using `trigger(...)`.\n1077: \n1078: The trigger interface WindowAssigner (Base Extension Point)\\n**Location:** `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/WindowAssigner.java`\\n**Class:** `public abstract class WindowAssigner<T, W extends Window>`\\n\\nDevelopers implementing custom window assignment must provide implementations for:\\n- `Collection<W> assignWindows(T element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context)` - Assigns zero or more windows to an element based on its timestamp\\n- `Trigger<T, W> getDefaultTrigger()` - Returns the default trigger for this window assigner\\n- `TypeSerializer<W> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig)` - Returns a serializer for the window type\\n- `boolean isEventTime()` - Indicates whether assignment is based on event time (true) or processing time (false)\\n\\nThe `WindowAssignerContext` inner class provides access to current processing time via `long getCurrentProcessingTime()`.\\n\\n### 2. MergingWindowAssigner (Session Window Extension Point)\\n**Location:** `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/MergingWindowAssigner.java`\\n**Class:** `public abstract class MergingWindowAssigner<T, W extends Window> extends WindowAssigner<T, W>`\\n\\nFor session-window scenarios where windows can be merged, this subclass adds:\\n- `void mergeWindows(Collection<W> windows, MergeCallback<W> callback)` - Determines which windows should be merged and invokes the callback with merge directives\\n- The `MergeCallback` interface allows implementations to signal: `void merge(Collection<W> toBeMerged, W mergeResult)` to specify which windows merge into which result window\\n\\n### 3. Trigger (Event Handling Extension Point)\\n**Location:** `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/Trigger.java`\\n**Class:** `public abstract class Trigger<T, W extends Window>`\\n\\nTriggers define when a pane should fire for output. The core lifecycle methods that must be implemented are:\\n- `TriggerResult onElement(T element, long timestamp, W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Called for each element added to a pane\\n- `TriggerResult onProcessingTime(long time, W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Called when a registered processing-time timer fires\\n- `TriggerResult onEventTime(long time, W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Called when a registered event-time timer fires\\n- `void clear(W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Cleanup handler when window is purged\\n\\nOptional methods for merging support (when used with `MergingWindowAssigner`):\\n- `boolean canMerge()` - Override to return true to enable merging support\\n- `void onMerge(W window, OnMergeContext ctx)` - Override to merge trigger state when windows are merged\\n\\nThe `TriggerContext` interface provides:\\n- Timer registration: `registerProcessingTimeTimer(long)`, `registerEventTimeTimer(long)`\\n- Timer cancellation: `deleteProcessingTimeTimer(long)`, `deleteEventTimeTimer(long)`\\n- State access: `<S extends State> S getPartitionedState(StateDescriptor<S, ?>)`\\n- Time queries: `long getCurrentProcessingTime()`, `long getCurrentWatermark()`\\n\\n### 4. EventTimeSessionWindows (Reference Implementation)\\n**Location:** `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/EventTimeSessionWindows.java`\\n**Class:** `public class EventTimeSessionWindows extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>`\\n\\nThis reference implementation demonstrates:\\n- **Constructor:** `EventTimeSessionWindows(long sessionTimeout)` - Stores session timeout in milliseconds\\n- **assignWindows():** Returns a single TimeWindow spanning from element timestamp to `timestamp + sessionTimeout`\\n  ```java\\n  return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(timestamp, timestamp + sessionTimeout));\\n  ```\\n- **mergeWindows():** Delegates to `TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c)` for overlapping window detection\\n- **getDefaultTrigger():** Returns `EventTimeTrigger.create()` for event-time driven evaluation\\n- **getWindowSerializer():** Returns `new TimeWindow.Serializer()` for serialization\\n- **isEventTime():** Returns `true` indicating event-time semantics\\n- Factory methods: `withGap(Duration)` and `withDynamicGap(SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor)` for creating instances\\n\\n### 5. TimeWindow (Output Type)\\n**Location:** `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/windows/TimeWindow.java`\\n**Class:** `public class TimeWindow extends Window`\\n\\nThe concrete window type produced by window assigners:\\n- **Constructor:** `TimeWindow(long start, long end)` - Represents interval from start (inclusive) to end (exclusive)\\n- **Accessors:**\\n  - `long getStart()` - Window start timestamp\\n  - `long getEnd()` - Exclusive window end timestamp\\n  - `long maxTimestamp()` - Returns `end - 1`, the last timestamp in the window\\n- **Window operations:**\\n  - `boolean intersects(TimeWindow other)` - Tests for window overlap\\n  - `TimeWindow cover(TimeWindow other)` - Creates minimal window covering both windows\\n- **Static utilities:**\\n  - `void mergeWindows(Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c)` - Sorts windows by start time and merges overlapping ones, invoking callback with merge instructions\\n  - `long getWindowStartWithOffset(long timestamp, long offset, long windowSize)` - Computes window start for a timestamp with optional offset\\n- **Serialization:** Inner `Serializer` class handles binary serialization (16 bytes: 8 for start, 8 for end)\\n\\n## Summary: Extension Point Chain\\n\\nThe extension architecture flows as:\\n1. A developer creates a custom `WindowAssigner` (or `MergingWindowAssigner` for session windows) implementing `assignWindows()` to emit window instances\\n2. The assigner creates concrete window objects (typically `TimeWindow` instances)\\n3. Each window pairing with a key creates a pane, governed by a `Trigger` implementation\\n4. The trigger's lifecycle methods (`onElement`, `onEventTime`, `onProcessingTime`, `onMerge`, `clear`) drive when panes fire\\n5. For session windows, `MergingWindowAssigner.mergeWindows()` and `Trigger.onMerge()` coordinate window consolidation\\n\\nThe reference implementation `EventTimeSessionWindows` shows the standard pattern: assigning overlapping session windows, delegating merge logic to the window class, and using a default trigger appropriate to the time semantics.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":5338,"cache_read_input_tokens":57387,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":5338},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"61c93c1a-78ca-4d78-9786-cbc9085a5261","uuid":"90cc7090-2f10-461b-bc19-1d545e13f74d"}
